effective-strategies.html

<p>Learning Arabic can be a deeply rewarding experience, but it also presents unique challenges. To make your journey smoother and more efficient, it's crucial to adopt smart learning strategies. Here are five proven techniques to help you learn Arabic faster.</p>
<h2>1. Master the Root System (Ø§Ù„Ø¬Ø°Ø±)</h2>
<p>The Arabic language is built on a system of three-letter roots. Understanding this system is like having a superpower. When you learn one root, you can often predict the meaning of a dozen related words. For example, the root <strong>Ùƒ-Øª-Ø¨ (k-t-b)</strong> relates to writing. From it, you get:</p>
<ul>
    <li><strong>ÙƒØªØ§Ø¨ (kitÄb)</strong> - book</li>
    <li><strong>ÙƒØ§ØªØ¨ (kÄtib)</strong> - writer</li>
    <li><strong>Ù…ÙƒØªØ¨ (maktab)</strong> - office/desk</li>
    <li><strong>Ù…ÙƒØªØ¨Ø© (maktabah)</strong> - library</li>
</ul>
<p>Focus on learning words in "root families" instead of as isolated items. This makes vocabulary acquisition more logical and much faster.</p>
<h2>2. Prioritize Active Recall and Spaced Repetition</h2>
<p>Passively reviewing flashcards is not enough. You need to actively test your brain. <strong>Active recall</strong> means trying to remember a word or concept without looking at the answer. Combine this with a <strong>Spaced Repetition System (SRS)</strong>, like Anki or Quizlet, which shows you information just before you're about to forget it. This method is scientifically proven to move information from your short-term to your long-term memory efficiently.</p>
<h2>3. Immerse Yourself in Comprehensible Input</h2>
<p>Surround yourself with Arabic that you can mostly understand. This is "comprehensible input." Don't jump into complex political news if you're a beginner. Instead, find materials slightly above your level:</p>
<ul>
    <li><strong>Beginners:</strong> Children's shows, graded readers, simple podcasts.</li>
    <li><strong>Intermediates:</strong> Vlogs on topics you enjoy, subtitled movies, daily news podcasts.</li>
</ul>
<p>The goal is to absorb the language naturally, focusing on understanding the message rather than analyzing every single word.</p>
<h2>4. Speak from Day One, Even if It's Just with Yourself</h2>
<p>Don't wait until you "feel ready" to speakâ€”you never will. Start speaking from the very first day. Describe objects around you, narrate your daily actions, or read texts aloud. The physical act of producing sounds builds muscle memory in your mouth and throat. A dedicated tutor, like those at Arabfield Academy, provides a safe space to practice, make mistakes, and get immediate feedback, which is the fastest way to build conversational fluency.</p>
<h2>5. Set Specific, Goal-Oriented Study Sessions</h2>
<p>Instead of a vague goal like "study Arabic for an hour," set a specific task. For example:</p>
<ol>
    <li>"Learn 10 new vocabulary words from the 'food' family and use each in a sentence."</li>
    <li>"Practice the past tense conjugation of three new verbs."</li>
    <li>"Listen to a 5-minute podcast and write a one-paragraph summary."</li>
</ol>
<p>This approach ensures your study time is focused and productive, leading to measurable progress and keeping you motivated.</p>



idafa-construction.html

<p>The <span class="arabic-term">Idafa (Ø§Ù„Ø¥Ø¶Ø§ÙØ©)</span> is one of the most fundamental and common grammatical structures in Arabic. Mastering it is a huge step towards sounding more natural and understanding complex sentences. In English, we call it the "possessive" or "genitive" construction. It's how you say things like "the door of the house" or "the student's book."</p>
<h2>The Two Parts of Idafa</h2>
<p>An Idafa construction consists of two (or more) nouns placed next to each other. The first noun is called the <span class="arabic-term">Ù…Ø¶Ø§Ù (muá¸Äf)</span>, and the second is the <span class="arabic-term">Ù…Ø¶Ø§Ù Ø¥Ù„ÙŠÙ‡ (muá¸Äf ilayhi)</span>.</p>
<ul>
    <li><strong>The Muá¸Äf (Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø¶Ø§Ù):</strong> The first noun, the thing that is "possessed."</li>
    <li><strong>The Muá¸Äf Ilayhi (Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø¶Ø§Ù Ø¥Ù„ÙŠÙ‡):</strong> The second noun, the "possessor."</li>
</ul>
<div class="example-box">
    <p class="arabic-example">Ø¨Ø§Ø¨Ù Ø§Ù„Ø¨ÙŠØªÙ</p>
    <p class="translation">(bÄbu l-bayti)</p>
    <p class="translation">The door of the house</p>
</div>
<p>In this example, "door" (Ø¨Ø§Ø¨) is the Muá¸Äf, and "the house" (Ø§Ù„Ø¨ÙŠØª) is the Muá¸Äf Ilayhi.</p>
<h2>The Three Rules of Idafa</h2>
<p>To form a correct Idafa, you just need to remember three simple rules that apply to the <strong>first noun (the Muá¸Äf)</strong>:</p>
<ol>
    <li><strong>It can NEVER have the definite article 'al-' (Ø§Ù„).</strong> It's always indefinite in form, but definite in meaning if the second noun is definite.</li>
    <li><strong>It can NEVER have tanween (Ù€ÙŒ, Ù€Ù, Ù€Ù‹).</strong> It takes only a single vowel at the end.</li>
    <li><strong>If it's a plural or dual, it drops its final 'n' (Ù†).</strong> For example, <span class="arabic-term">Ù…Ø¹Ù„Ù…ÙˆÙ†</span> (teachers) becomes <span class="arabic-term">Ù…Ø¹Ù„Ù…Ùˆ</span> in an Idafa.</li>
</ol>
<p>The <strong>second noun (the Muá¸Äf Ilayhi)</strong> has only one rule: it must always be in the genitive case (Ù…Ø¬Ø±ÙˆØ±), which usually means it ends in <em>kasra</em> (Ù) or <em>kasratain</em> (Ù).</p>
<h2>More Examples</h2>
<div class="example-box">
    <p class="arabic-example">ÙƒØªØ§Ø¨Ù Ø·Ø§Ù„Ø¨Ù</p>
    <p class="translation">(kitÄbu á¹­Älibin)</p>
    <p class="translation">A student's book (the book of a student)</p>
</div>
<div class="example-box">
    <p class="arabic-example">Ù…ÙØªØ§Ø­Ù Ø§Ù„Ø³ÙŠØ§Ø±Ø©Ù</p>
    <p class="translation">(miftÄá¸¥u s-sayyÄrati)</p>
    <p class="translation">The key of the car</p>
</div>
<div class="example-box">
    <p class="arabic-example">Ù…ÙØ¯ÙŠØ±Ù Ø§Ù„Ø´Ø±ÙƒØ©Ù</p>
    <p class="translation">(mudÄ«ru sh-sharikati)</p>
    <p class="translation">The manager of the company</p>
</div>
<p>Once you start recognizing the Idafa pattern, you'll see it everywhere in Arabic. Practicing it will dramatically improve your ability to read and form more complex and elegant sentences.</p>

mastering-pronunciation.html

<p>Arabic pronunciation can be one of the most challenging aspects for non-native speakers. The language features unique sounds not found in English or many other European languages, requiring dedicated practice and a keen ear. However, with the right techniques and consistent effort, you can achieve clear and confident Arabic pronunciation.</p>

<h2>Understanding Unique Arabic Sounds</h2>
<p>Before diving into practice, it's crucial to identify the sounds that are most likely to cause difficulty. These often include:</p>
<ul>
    <li><strong>Guttural Sounds:</strong> Such as the letters Ø­ (á¸¥ÄÊ¾), Ø¹ (Ê¿ayn), Øº (ghayn), and Ø® (khÄÊ¾). These are produced deep in the throat.</li>
    <li><strong>Emphatic Consonants:</strong> Like Øµ (á¹£Äd), Ø¶ (á¸Äd), Ø· (á¹­ÄÊ¾), and Ø¸ (áº“ÄÊ¾). These are pronounced with the back of the tongue raised towards the soft palate, giving them a 'heavy' sound.</li>
    <li><strong>The Letter Ù‚ (qÄf):</strong> A deep, uvular stop that is often confused with 'k' by beginners.</li>
</ul>

<h2>Tips for Improvement</h2>
<p>Here are some practical tips to help you master these sounds and improve your overall Arabic pronunciation:</p>
<ol>
    <li><strong>Listen Actively:</strong> Pay close attention to native speakers. Listen to Arabic podcasts, news, songs, and watch movies. Try to mimic the sounds you hear. Repetition is key.</li>
    <li><strong>Practice Minimal Pairs:</strong> These are pairs of words that differ by only one sound (e.g., 'Ù‚ÙŽÙ„Ù’Ø¨' (qalb - heart) vs. 'ÙƒÙŽÙ„Ù’Ø¨' (kalb - dog)). Practicing them helps you distinguish and produce subtle sound differences.</li>
    <li><strong>Record Yourself:</strong> Use your phone or computer to record your speech. Listen back and compare it to a native speaker's pronunciation. This helps you identify areas for improvement.</li>
    <li><strong>Focus on Articulation:</strong> Understand where each sound is produced in your mouth and throat. Many online resources and textbooks provide detailed diagrams and explanations of Arabic phonetics.</li>
    <li><strong>Work with a Native Speaker Tutor:</strong> The most effective way to improve pronunciation is to get direct feedback from a native speaker. A tutor can correct your mistakes in real-time and guide you through difficult sounds.</li>
</ol>

<p>Mastering Arabic pronunciation takes time and dedication, but the rewards are immense. Clear pronunciation not only makes you easier to understand but also boosts your confidence in speaking the language.</p>

staying-motivated.html

<p>Every language learner hits a plateau. The initial excitement fades, progress seems to slow down, and motivation can plummet. This is a completely normal part of the process. The key to success is not to avoid these moments, but to have strategies in place to push through them. Hereâ€™s how to stay motivated on your Arabic learning journey.</p>

<p>Take a moment to remember why you started learning Arabic in the first place. Was it to connect with family? For a career opportunity? To read the Quran in its original language? To travel and immerse yourself in a new culture? Write down your core motivation and place it somewhere you can see it every day. When you feel discouraged, revisiting your "why" can reignite your passion.</p>
<h2>2. Set Small, Achievable Goals</h2>
<p>A goal like "become fluent in Arabic" is huge and intimidating. It can make you feel like you're not making any progress. Instead, break it down into small, weekly goals. For example:</p>
<ul>
    <li>"This week, I will learn 15 new words related to food."</li>
    <li>"I will have a 5-minute conversation with my tutor about my weekend."</li>
    <li>"I will watch one episode of a simple Arabic cartoon."</li>

<h2>4. Track Your Progress</h2>
<p>It's easy to forget how far you've come. Keep a learning journal. Once a month, look back at your notes or recordings from when you started. You'll be amazed at your progress. <h2>5. Find a Community or a Partner</h2>

They provide not just instruction, but also encouragement and accountability. You can also join online forums or language exchange apps to connect with other learners who understand your struggles and can celebrate your victories.</p>
<p>Remember, motivation is not a constant; it's a wave. The trick is to build good habits that carry you through the low points until the next wave of inspiration arrives.</p>



sun-moon-letters.html

<p>One of the first pronunciation rules you'll encounter in Arabic is the curious case of the definite article 'al-' (Ø§Ù„). Sometimes the 'l' sound is pronounced clearly, and other times it disappears, causing the next letter to be doubled. This is all determined by whether the letter following 'al-' is a "sun letter" or a "moon letter."</p>
<h2>What are Moon Letters (Ø§Ù„Ø­Ø±ÙˆÙ Ø§Ù„Ù‚Ù…Ø±ÙŠØ©)?</h2>
<p>Moon letters are the "easy" ones. When the definite article 'al-' comes before a moon letter, the 'l' (Ù„) is pronounced clearly and distinctly. The name comes from the word for "the moon," <span class="arabic-term">Ø§Ù„Ù‚Ù…Ø± (al-qamar)</span>, where you can clearly hear the 'l' sound.</p>
<p>There are 14 moon letters.</p>
<h2>What are Sun Letters (Ø§Ù„Ø­Ø±ÙˆÙ Ø§Ù„Ø´Ù…Ø³ÙŠØ©)?</h2>
<p>Sun letters are the "tricky" ones. When 'al-' comes before a sun letter, the 'l' sound is NOT pronounced. Instead, it assimilates into the sun letter, which is then stressed or doubled (indicated by a <em>shadda</em> Ù‘ symbol in writing). The name comes from the word for "the sun," <span class="arabic-term">Ø§Ù„Ø´Ù…Ø³ (ash-shams)</span>, where the 'l' is silent and the 'sh' sound is doubled.</p>
<p>There are also 14 sun letters.</p>
<h2>The Complete List</h2>

    <thead>
        <tr>
            <th class="moon-header">Moon Letters (14)</th>
            <th class="sun-header">Sun Letters (14)</th>
        </tr>
    </thead>
    <tbody>
        <tr>
            <td>Ø£ ØŒ Ø¨ ØŒ Ø¬ ØŒ Ø­ ØŒ Ø® ØŒ Ø¹ ØŒ Øº ØŒ Ù ØŒ Ù‚ ØŒ Ùƒ ØŒ Ù… ØŒ Ù‡Ù€ ØŒ Ùˆ ØŒ ÙŠ</td>
            <td>Øª ØŒ Ø« ØŒ Ø¯ ØŒ Ø° ØŒ Ø± ØŒ Ø² ØŒ Ø³ ØŒ Ø´ ØŒ Øµ ØŒ Ø¶ ØŒ Ø· ØŒ Ø¸ ØŒ Ù„ ØŒ Ù†</td>
        </tr>
    </tbody>
</table>
<h2>Why Does This Matter?</h2>
<p>Mastering this rule is crucial for correct pronunciation and will make your spoken Arabic sound much more natural and fluent. It's one of the key indicators that separates a beginner from an intermediate speaker. While it might seem like a lot to memorize, you'll find that with listening and speaking practice, it will become second nature.</p>



verb-conjugation.html

<p>For many beginners, Arabic verb conjugation seems like a monumental task. However, unlike the irregular verbs of English, Arabic verbs follow a highly logical and predictable pattern-based system. Once you understand the core concepts of root and pattern, conjugation becomes a skill you can master.</p>
<h2>The Root and Pattern System</h2>
<p>Most Arabic verbs are derived from a three-letter <strong>root (Ø¬Ø°Ø±)</strong> that carries a core meaning. For example, <strong>Ù-Ø¹-Ù„ (f-'-l)</strong> means "to do." This root is then placed into different <strong>patterns (Ø£ÙˆØ²Ø§Ù†)</strong> to create different meanings and tenses.</p>
<p>We'll use the simplest pattern, Form I, for our examples.</p>
<h2>Past Tense (Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø§Ø¶ÙŠ - al-mÄá¸Ä«)</h2>
<p>The past tense is formed by adding suffixes to the end of the verb root. These suffixes indicate the person, gender, and number of the subject.</p>
<p>Let's conjugate <strong>ÙƒÙŽØªÙŽØ¨ÙŽ (kataba - he wrote)</strong>:</p>
<ul>
    <li>I wrote: <strong>ÙƒØªØ¨ØªÙ (katabtu)</strong></li>
    <li>You (m.) wrote: <strong>ÙƒØªØ¨ØªÙŽ (katabta)</strong></li>
    <li>You (f.) wrote: <strong>ÙƒØªØ¨ØªÙ (katabti)</strong></li>
    <li>He wrote: <strong>ÙƒØªØ¨ÙŽ (kataba)</strong></li>
    <li>She wrote: <strong>ÙƒØªØ¨ÙŽØªÙ’ (katabat)</strong></li>
    <li>We wrote: <strong>ÙƒØªØ¨Ù†Ø§ (katabnÄ)</strong></li>
    <li>They wrote: <strong>ÙƒØªØ¨ÙˆØ§ (katabÅ«)</strong></li>
</ul>
<h2>Present Tense (Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø¶Ø§Ø±Ø¹ - al-muá¸Äri')</h2>
<p>The present tense is formed by adding both prefixes and suffixes. The prefixes are the most important part for identifying the subject.</p>
<p>Let's conjugate <strong>ÙŠÙƒØªØ¨ (yaktubu - he writes)</strong>:</p>
<ul>
    <li>I write: <strong>Ø£ÙƒØªØ¨ (aktubu)</strong> - Prefix 'Ø£'</li>
    <li>You (m.) write: <strong>ØªÙƒØªØ¨ (taktubu)</strong> - Prefix 'Øª'</li>
    <li>You (f.) write: <strong>ØªÙƒØªØ¨ÙŠÙ† (taktubÄ«na)</strong> - Prefix 'Øª' and Suffix 'ÙŠÙ†'</li>
    <li>He writes: <strong>ÙŠÙƒØªØ¨ (yaktubu)</strong> - Prefix 'ÙŠ'</li>
    <li>She writes: <strong>ØªÙƒØªØ¨ (taktubu)</strong> - Prefix 'Øª' (same as "you m.")</li>
    <li>We write: <strong>Ù†ÙƒØªØ¨ (naktubu)</strong> - Prefix 'Ù†'</li>
    <li>They write: <strong>ÙŠÙƒØªØ¨ÙˆÙ† (yaktubÅ«na)</strong> - Prefix 'ÙŠ' and Suffix 'ÙˆÙ†'</li>
</ul>
<h2>Tips for Mastery</h2>
<p>Don't try to memorize every conjugation for every verb. Instead, focus on memorizing the <strong>patterns of suffixes and prefixes</strong>. Practice with common verbs like ÙƒØªØ¨ (to write), Ù‚Ø±Ø£ (to read), and Ø°Ù‡Ø¨ (to go). With consistent practice, the patterns will become automatic.</p>



vocabulary-roots.html

<p>If there is one "hack" to learning Arabic vocabulary efficiently, it's understanding the three-letter root system. The vast majority of Arabic words are built from a root (usually three consonants) that holds a core concept. By learning this single root, you can unlock the meaning of a whole family of related words.</p>
<h2>How Does It Work?</h2>
<p>Think of the root as the DNA of a word. By adding vowels and other letters in specific, predictable patterns (Ø£ÙˆØ²Ø§Ù† - awzÄn), new words are formed, all connected to the root's original meaning.</p>
<h2>Example: The Root Ø¯-Ø±-Ø³ (d-r-s)</h2>
<p>This root carries the core concept of "to study" or "to learn." Look at how many words you can understand just by knowing this one root:</p>
<ul>
    <li><strong>Ø¯ÙŽØ±ÙŽØ³ÙŽ (darasa)</strong> - He studied (the basic verb)</li>
    <li><strong>ÙŠÙŽØ¯Ø±ÙØ³ (yadrusu)</strong> - He studies (present tense verb)</li>
    <li><strong>Ø¯ÙØ±Ø§Ø³Ø© (dirÄsah)</strong> - Studying; a study (the concept)</li>
    <li><strong>Ø¯ÙŽØ±Ø³ (dars)</strong> - A lesson</li>
    <li><strong>Ù…ÙŽØ¯Ø±ÙŽØ³Ø© (madrasah)</strong> - School (the place of studying)</li>
    <li><strong>Ù…ÙØ¯ÙŽØ±Ù‘ÙØ³ (mudarris)</strong> - A teacher (the one who causes others to study)</li>
    <li><strong>ØªÙŽØ¯Ø±ÙŠØ³ (tadrÄ«s)</strong> - Teaching (the act of causing others to study)</li>
</ul>
<p>By learning one root, you've just learned seven related words! This is far more effective than memorizing seven random words from a list.</p>
<h2>Another Example: The Root Ø¹-Ù„-Ù… ('-l-m)</h2>
<p>This root relates to "knowing" or "knowledge."</p>
<ul>
    <li><strong>Ø¹ÙŽÙ„ÙÙ…ÙŽ (Ê¿alima)</strong> - He knew</li>
    <li><strong>Ø¹ÙÙ„Ù… (Ê¿ilm)</strong> - Science, knowledge</li>
    <li><strong>Ø¹Ø§Ù„ÙÙ… (Ê¿Älim)</strong> - A scholar, a scientist (one who knows)</li>
    <li><strong>Ù…ÙŽØ¹Ù„ÙˆÙ…Ø§Øª (maÊ¿lÅ«mÄt)</strong> - Information (things that are known)</li>
    <li><strong>Ø¹ÙŽÙ„Ù‘ÙŽÙ…ÙŽ (Ê¿allama)</strong> - He taught (he made someone know)</li>
    <li><strong>Ù…ÙØ¹ÙŽÙ„Ù‘ÙÙ… (muÊ¿allim)</strong> - A teacher (one who teaches)</li>
</ul>
<h2>How to Use This Strategy</h2>
<p>When you learn a new word, ask your tutor or look in a dictionary for its three-letter root. Keep a notebook organized by roots instead of alphabetically. As you encounter new words, add them to the correct "root family." This will transform your vocabulary learning from a memory game into a logical puzzle, making it faster, easier, and much more rewarding.</p>

rate-limiter.js

// rate-limiter.js
class RateLimiter {
    constructor() {
        this.limits = new Map();
        setInterval(() => this.cleanup(), 60000);
    }
    
    check(ip, maxRequests = 100, windowMs = 900000) {
        const now = Date.now();
        const key = `rate_${ip}`;
        let requests = this.limits.get(key) || [];
        requests = requests.filter(time => now - time < windowMs);
        
        if (requests.length >= maxRequests) return false;
        
        requests.push(now);
        this.limits.set(key, requests);
        return true;
    }
}

recovery.js


// recovery.js - Ù†Ø¸Ø§Ù… Ø§Ù„Ø§Ø³ØªØ¹Ø§Ø¯Ø© ÙˆØ§Ù„ØªØ¹Ø§ÙÙŠ
class SystemRecovery {
    constructor() {
        this.backupInterval = 6 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 6 Ø³Ø§Ø¹Ø§Øª
        this.maxAutoBackups = 10;
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.setupAutoBackup();
        this.setupErrorRecovery();
        this.setupDataValidation();
    }

    setupAutoBackup() {
        // Ù†Ø³Ø® Ø§Ø­ØªÙŠØ§Ø·ÙŠ ØªÙ„Ù‚Ø§Ø¦ÙŠ ÙƒÙ„ 6 Ø³Ø§Ø¹Ø§Øª
        setInterval(() => {
            this.createAutoBackup();
        }, this.backupInterval);

        // Ù†Ø³Ø® Ø§Ø­ØªÙŠØ§Ø·ÙŠ Ù‚Ø¨Ù„ Ø¥ØºÙ„Ø§Ù‚ Ø§Ù„ØµÙØ­Ø©
        window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
            this.createQuickBackup();
        });
    }

    createAutoBackup() {
        const backupData = {
            type: 'auto_backup',
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            data: {
                session: this.getSessionData(),
                userData: this.getUserData(),
                forms: this.getFormsData()
            }
        };

        this.saveBackup(backupData);
        this.cleanupOldBackups();

        if (window.logger) {
            window.logger.info('Auto backup created', { timestamp: backupData.timestamp });
        }
    }

    createQuickBackup() {
        const criticalData = {
            type: 'quick_backup',
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            data: {
                sessionId: sessionStorage.getItem('session_id'),
                formData: this.getUnsavedFormData(),
                currentPage: window.location.href
            }
        };

        localStorage.setItem('last_quick_backup', JSON.stringify(criticalData));
    }

    getSessionData() {
        return {
            sessionId: sessionStorage.getItem('session_id'),
            lastActivity: sessionStorage.getItem('last_activity'),
            userPreferences: this.getUserPreferences()
        };
    }

    getUserData() {
        return {
            userId: localStorage.getItem('ara_user_id'),
            chatHistory: JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ara_chat_history') || '[]'),
            bookings: JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ara_bookings') || '[]')
        };
    }

    getFormsData() {
        // Ø­ÙØ¸ Ø¨ÙŠØ§Ù†Ø§Øª Ø§Ù„Ù†Ù…Ø§Ø°Ø¬ ØºÙŠØ± Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø³Ù„Ù…Ø©
        const formsData = {};
        document.querySelectorAll('form').forEach((form, index) => {
            const formData = new FormData(form);
            const data = {};
            for (let [key, value] of formData.entries()) {
                data[key] = value;
            }
            if (Object.keys(data).length > 0) {
                formsData[form.id || `form_${index}`] = data;
            }
        });
        return formsData;
    }

    getUnsavedFormData() {
        const unsavedData = {};
        document.querySelectorAll('input, textarea, select').forEach(field => {
            if (field.value && field.value !== field.defaultValue) {
                unsavedData[field.name] = field.value;
            }
        });
        return unsavedData;
    }

    getUserPreferences() {
        const prefs = {};
        for (let i = 0; i < localStorage.length; i++) {
            const key = localStorage.key(i);
            if (key.startsWith('user_pref_') || key.startsWith('ara_')) {
                prefs[key] = localStorage.getItem(key);
            }
        }
        return prefs;
    }

    saveBackup(backupData) {
        const backups = this.getBackups();
        backups.push(backupData);
        localStorage.setItem('system_backups', JSON.stringify(backups));
    }

    getBackups() {
        try {
            return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('system_backups') || '[]');
        } catch {
            return [];
        }
    }

    cleanupOldBackups() {
        const backups = this.getBackups();
        const autoBackups = backups.filter(b => b.type === 'auto_backup');
        
        if (autoBackups.length > this.maxAutoBackups) {
            const recentBackups = autoBackups.slice(-this.maxAutoBackups);
            const otherBackups = backups.filter(b => b.type !== 'auto_backup');
            const allBackups = [...otherBackups, ...recentBackups];
            localStorage.setItem('system_backups', JSON.stringify(allBackups));
        }
    }

    setupErrorRecovery() {
        // Ø§Ø³ØªØ¹Ø§Ø¯Ø© Ù…Ù† Ø¢Ø®Ø± Ù†Ø³Ø®Ø© Ø¹Ù†Ø¯ ÙˆØ¬ÙˆØ¯ Ø£Ø®Ø·Ø§Ø¡
        window.addEventListener('error', () => {
            setTimeout(() => {
                this.attemptRecovery();
            }, 1000);
        });

        // Ø§Ø³ØªØ¹Ø§Ø¯Ø© Ø¹Ù†Ø¯ ÙØ´Ù„ ØªØ­Ù…ÙŠÙ„ Ø§Ù„ØµÙØ­Ø©
        window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', (e) => {
            if (e.reason instanceof TypeError) {
                this.attemptRecovery();
            }
        });
    }

    attemptRecovery() {
        const lastBackup = localStorage.getItem('last_quick_backup');
        if (lastBackup) {
            try {
                const backup = JSON.parse(lastBackup);
                this.restoreFromBackup(backup);
            } catch (e) {
                console.warn('Recovery failed:', e);
            }
        }
    }

    restoreFromBackup(backup) {
        console.log('ðŸ”„ Attempting recovery from backup:', backup.timestamp);

        // Ø§Ø³ØªØ¹Ø§Ø¯Ø© Ø¨ÙŠØ§Ù†Ø§Øª Ø§Ù„Ø¬Ù„Ø³Ø©
        if (backup.data.sessionId) {
            sessionStorage.setItem('session_id', backup.data.sessionId);
        }

        // Ø§Ø³ØªØ¹Ø§Ø¯Ø© Ø¨ÙŠØ§Ù†Ø§Øª Ø§Ù„Ù†Ù…Ø§Ø°Ø¬
        if (backup.data.formData) {
            this.restoreFormData(backup.data.formData);
        }

        if (window.logger) {
            window.logger.info('System recovery attempted', { 
                timestamp: backup.timestamp,
                success: true 
            });
        }
    }

    restoreFormData(formData) {
        Object.keys(formData).forEach(fieldName => {
            const field = document.querySelector(`[name="${fieldName}"]`);
            if (field && field.value === '') {
                field.value = formData[fieldName];
            }
        });
    }

    setupDataValidation() {
        // Ø§Ù„ØªØ­Ù‚Ù‚ Ù…Ù† Ø³Ù„Ø§Ù…Ø© Ø§Ù„Ø¨ÙŠØ§Ù†Ø§Øª Ø¨Ø§Ù†ØªØ¸Ø§Ù…
        setInterval(() => {
            this.validateStoredData();
        }, 30 * 60 * 1000); // ÙƒÙ„ 30 Ø¯Ù‚ÙŠÙ‚Ø©
    }

    validateStoredData() {
        let issues = 0;

        // Ø§Ù„ØªØ­Ù‚Ù‚ Ù…Ù† Ø¨ÙŠØ§Ù†Ø§Øª Ø§Ù„Ø­Ø¬ÙˆØ²Ø§Øª
        try {
            const bookings = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ara_bookings') || '[]');
            if (!Array.isArray(bookings)) {
                localStorage.setItem('ara_bookings', '[]');
                issues++;
            }
        } catch {
            localStorage.setItem('ara_bookings', '[]');
            issues++;
        }

        // Ø§Ù„ØªØ­Ù‚Ù‚ Ù…Ù† Ø³Ø¬Ù„ Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø¯Ø«Ø©
        try {
            const chatHistory = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ara_chat_history') || '[]');
            if (!Array.isArray(chatHistory)) {
                localStorage.setItem('ara_chat_history', '[]');
                issues++;
            }
        } catch {
            localStorage.setItem('ara_chat_history', '[]');
            issues++;
        }

        if (issues > 0 && window.logger) {
            window.logger.warn('Data validation found issues', { issuesCount: issues });
        }

        return issues === 0;
    }

    // Ø§Ø³ØªØ¹Ø§Ø¯Ø© ÙƒØ§Ù…Ù„Ø© Ù„Ù„Ù†Ø¸Ø§Ù…
    fullSystemRecovery() {
        const backups = this.getBackups();
        const latestBackup = backups[backups.length - 1];
        
        if (latestBackup) {
            this.restoreFromBackup(latestBackup);
            return true;
        }
        return false;
    }

    // Ø¥Ø¹Ø§Ø¯Ø© ØªØ¹ÙŠÙŠÙ† Ø§Ù„Ù†Ø¸Ø§Ù…
    resetSystem() {
        if (confirm('Are you sure you want to reset all system data? This cannot be undone.')) {
            localStorage.clear();
            sessionStorage.clear();
            window.location.reload();
        }
    }

    getRecoveryStatus() {
        const backups = this.getBackups();
        const lastBackup = backups[backups.length - 1];
        const dataValid = this.validateStoredData();

        return {
            hasBackups: backups.length > 0,
            lastBackup: lastBackup?.timestamp,
            totalBackups: backups.length,
            dataIntegrity: dataValid,
            quickBackup: localStorage.getItem('last_quick_backup') !== null
        };
    }
}

if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
    window.SystemRecovery = SystemRecovery;
}

// Ø¨Ø§Ù‚ÙŠ Ø§Ù„Ø¯ÙˆØ§Ù„ ØªØ¨Ù‚Ù‰ ÙƒÙ…Ø§ Ù‡ÙŠ...
async function loadTemplates() {
    const templates = [
        { id: "main-header-placeholder", file: "templates/header.html" },
        { id: "main-footer-placeholder", file: "templates/footer.html" },
        { id: "fabs-placeholder", file: "templates/fabs.html" },
        { id: "modal-placeholder", file: "templates/contact-modal.html" }
    ];
    
    for (const template of templates) {
        await loadTemplate(template.id, template.file);
    }
}

async function loadTemplate(elementId, templateFile) {
    try {
        const element = document.getElementById(elementId);
        if (!element) return;
        
        const response = await fetch(templateFile);
        if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to load: ${templateFile}`);
        
        element.innerHTML = await response.text();
        processLoadedTemplate(element);
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Template loading error:', error);
    }
}

function processLoadedTemplate(element) {
    // ØªØ£Ù…ÙŠÙ† Ø§Ù„Ø±ÙˆØ§Ø¨Ø· ÙˆØ§Ù„ØµÙˆØ± ÙÙŠ Ø§Ù„Ù‚ÙˆØ§Ù„Ø¨ Ø§Ù„Ù…Ø­Ù…Ù„Ø©
    element.querySelectorAll('a').forEach(link => {
        const href = link.getAttribute('href');
        if (href && !href.startsWith('http') && !href.startsWith('#') && !href.startsWith('mailto:')) {
            link.href = href;
        }
    });
    
    element.querySelectorAll('img').forEach(img => {
        const src = img.getAttribute('src');
        if (src && !src.startsWith('http')) {
            img.src = src;
        }
    });
}

function initializeComponents() {
    // ØªÙ‡ÙŠØ¦Ø© AOS Ù„Ù„Ø§Ù†ÙŠÙ…ÙŠØ´Ù†
    if (typeof AOS !== 'undefined') {
        AOS.init({
            duration: 800,
            easing: 'ease-in-out',
            once: true
        });
    }
    
    // ØªÙ‡ÙŠØ¦Ø© FAQ accordion
    initializeFAQ();
    
    // ØªÙ‡ÙŠØ¦Ø© Ù†Ù…Ø§Ø°Ø¬ Ø§Ù„Ø§ØªØµØ§Ù„
    initializeForms();
}

function initializeFAQ() {
    const faqItems = document.querySelectorAll('.faq-item');
    faqItems.forEach(item => {
        const question = item.querySelector('.faq-question');
        question.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const currentlyActive = document.querySelector('.faq-item.active');
            if (currentlyActive && currentlyActive !== item) {
                currentlyActive.classList.remove('active');
            }
            item.classList.toggle('active');
        });
    });
}

function initializeForms() {
    const forms = document.querySelectorAll('form');
    forms.forEach(form => {
        form.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            // Ø§Ù„Ø­Ù…Ø§ÙŠØ© ØªØªÙ… Ø¹Ø¨Ø± AuthMiddleware ØªÙ„Ù‚Ø§Ø¦ÙŠØ§Ù‹
            console.log('Form submission protected by security system');
        });
    });
}

function startServices() {
    // Ø¨Ø¯Ø¡ Ø§Ù„Ø®Ø¯Ù…Ø§Øª Ø§Ù„Ø¥Ø¶Ø§ÙÙŠØ©
    startLazyLoading();
    startPerformanceMonitoring();
    
    console.log('âœ… All application services started');
}

function startLazyLoading() {
    const lazyImages = document.querySelectorAll('img[loading="lazy"]');
    const observer = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach(entry => {
            if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                const img = entry.target;
                img.src = img.src;
                img.classList.add('loaded');
                observer.unobserve(img);
            }
        });
    });
    
    lazyImages.forEach(img => observer.observe(img));
}

function startPerformanceMonitoring() {
    // Ù…Ø±Ø§Ù‚Ø¨Ø© Ø§Ù„Ø£Ø¯Ø§Ø¡ Ø¨Ø´ÙƒÙ„ Ù…Ø¨Ø³Ø·
    window.addEventListener('load', () => {
        const loadTime = performance.timing.loadEventEnd - performance.timing.navigationStart;
        if (window.analytics) {
            window.analytics.trackEvent('performance', 'page_load_time', null, loadTime);
        }
    });
}

// Ø¯Ø§Ù„Ø© Ù…Ø³Ø§Ø¹Ø¯Ø© Ù„Ù„Ø±ÙˆØ§Ø¨Ø·
function resolveUrl(url) {
    if (!url || url.startsWith("http") || url.startsWith("#") || url.startsWith("mailto:")) {
        return url;
    }
    return url;
}

// security-integration.js - ØªÙƒØ§Ù…Ù„ Ø§Ù„Ø£Ù†Ø¸Ù…Ø©
class SecurityIntegration {
    constructor() {
        this.integrated = false;
        this.init();
    }
    
    init() {
        this.integrateWithExistingSystems();
        this.setupGlobalProtection();
        this.monitorIntegration();
    }
    
    integrateWithExistingSystems() {
        // Ø§Ù„ØªÙƒØ§Ù…Ù„ Ù…Ø¹ analytics
        if (window.analytics) {
            this.patchAnalytics();
        }
        
        // Ø§Ù„ØªÙƒØ§Ù…Ù„ Ù…Ø¹ booking system
        if (window.bookingSystem) {
            this.patchBookingSystem();
        }
        
        // Ø§Ù„ØªÙƒØ§Ù…Ù„ Ù…Ø¹ live chat
        if (window.liveChat) {
            this.patchLiveChat();
        }
        
        this.integrated = true;
        console.log('âœ… Security systems integrated successfully');
    }
    
    patchAnalytics() {
        const originalTrack = window.analytics.trackEvent;
        window.analytics.trackEvent = function(category, action, label, value) {
            // ØªØ³Ø¬ÙŠÙ„ Ø£Ø­Ø¯Ø§Ø« Ø§Ù„Ø£Ù…Ø§Ù†
            if (category === 'security') {
                if (window.logger) {
                    window.logger.security(`${action}: ${label}`);
                }
            }
            return originalTrack.call(this, category, action, label, value);
        };
    }
    
    patchBookingSystem() {
        if (window.bookingSystem && window.bookingSystem.confirmBooking) {
            const originalConfirm = window.bookingSystem.confirmBooking;
            window.bookingSystem.confirmBooking = function(slotId, formData) {
                // Ø§Ù„ØªØ­Ù‚Ù‚ Ø§Ù„Ø£Ù…Ù†ÙŠ Ù‚Ø¨Ù„ Ø§Ù„Ø­Ø¬Ø²
                if (!validateFormSecurity(this)) {
                    return false;
                }
                return originalConfirm.call(this, slotId, formData);
            };
        }
    }
    
    patchLiveChat() {
        if (window.liveChat && window.liveChat.sendMessage) {
            const originalSend = window.liveChat.sendMessage;
            window.liveChat.sendMessage = function() {
                // Ø§Ù„ØªØ­Ù‚Ù‚ Ù…Ù† Ù…Ø­ØªÙˆÙ‰ Ø§Ù„Ø±Ø³Ø§Ù„Ø©
                const input = document.getElementById('chatInput');
                if (input && !validateUserInput(input.value)) {
                    alert('Message contains suspicious content');
                    return;
                }
                return originalSend.call(this);
            };
        }
    }
    
    setupGlobalProtection() {
        // Ù…Ø±Ø§Ù‚Ø¨Ø© Ø§Ù„ØªØºÙŠÙŠØ±Ø§Øª ÙÙŠ DOM
        this.monitorDOMMutations();
    }
    
    monitorDOMMutations() {
        const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
            mutations.forEach((mutation) => {
                mutation.addedNodes.forEach((node) => {
                    if (node.nodeType === 1) {
                        this.checkSuspiciousElement(node);
                    }
                });
            });
        });
        
        observer.observe(document.body, {
            childList: true,
            subtree: true
        });
    }
    
    checkSuspiciousElement(element) {
        const suspiciousPatterns = [
            /<script/i,
            /javascript:/i,
            /on\w+=/i
        ];
        
        const html = element.outerHTML || element.innerHTML || '';
        suspiciousPatterns.forEach(pattern => {
            if (pattern.test(html)) {
                console.warn('ðŸš¨ Suspicious element detected:', element);
            }
        });
    }
    
    monitorIntegration() {
        setInterval(() => {
            this.checkIntegrationHealth();
        }, 30000);
    }
    
    checkIntegrationHealth() {
        const health = {
            securitySystem: !!window.securitySystem,
            analytics: !!window.analytics,
            booking: !!window.bookingSystem,
            chat: !!window.liveChat,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        };
        
        return health;
    }
}

// Ø¯ÙˆØ§Ù„ Ù…Ø³Ø§Ø¹Ø¯Ø©
function validateFormSecurity(form) {
    const honeypot = form.querySelector('input[name="user_website"]');
    if (honeypot && honeypot.value) return false;
    
    const tokenInput = form.querySelector('input[name="_security_token"]');
    if (tokenInput) {
        const storedToken = sessionStorage.getItem('form_token');
        if (!storedToken || storedToken !== tokenInput.value) return false;
    }
    
    return true;
}

function validateUserInput(input) {
    if (!input) return true;
    const dangerousPatterns = [/<script/i, /javascript:/i, /on\w+=/i];
    return !dangerousPatterns.some(pattern => pattern.test(input));
}

if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
    window.SecurityIntegration = SecurityIntegration;
}
